Minibosses level 1-19 have an increased chance of dropping items. Every minute, a random item spawns in the center of the map. It can be a rune of dexterity/mind/strength/experience or a neutral item. The level of neutral items depends on the time of the game. At 5 minutes Divine Rapier appears in the center of the map."

If you enter the zone to the epic bosses without killing the megaboss, then you will begin to receive periodic damage. All megabosses have a teleport to epic bosses. Phoenix unlocks the epic boss Lina. Tide to Morphling. Broodmother to Venomancer. Ancient Apparition to Lich."
